msg:This is a hotel that deserves my highest rating.
The hotel is located in a quieter corner near the south gate of Lijiang Old Town.
I took an early flight to Lijiang and booked a hotel pick-up service. I arrived at the hotel at 11 o'clock. I thought I would have to find a place to rest and wait for check-in, but the hotel staff served me tea and snacks and explained the hotel facilities and meals. After the incident, our luggage was sent to the room and we were arranged to check in immediately. This was very gratifying for us who rushed to the airport at 5 o'clock in the morning.
The interior and exterior decoration of the hotel is simple and elegant. I like that it doesn't have any unnecessary tricks, but everything is in place. The room is beautiful, with an elegant bookish feel. The room is of a reasonable size and there is no shortage of space. The bathroom decoration is simple and in place. The toiletries included are all branded. The waiter said that they have three brands to choose from. , if you don‚Äôt like the brand you have arranged now, you can inform them to change it. I especially like its metal wash basin, which is like a "ringing bell". When you ring it gently, there will be a low and ethereal ringing, which makes the mind and body peaceful.
It must be mentioned that the front desk staff, catering staff, and housekeepers are all very friendly and courteous. They not only answer questions patiently, but also try their best to satisfy requests as quickly as possible. Since the front desk is right next to the entrance, they will greet you every time you come back. "We're back~". If it's early, they'll say "You can eat some fruit and then go back to your room to rest." If it's late, they'll say "You're tired, have a good rest." It really feels warm. On the day we left, we wanted to borrow the hotel's trolley to pull our luggage to the intersection. A hotel lady took the initiative to help us pull it out. When we were waiting for the driver to pick us up, we wanted to take the luggage and let her go back, but she only asked us to sit down. After waiting, she stood beside the cart under the bright sun and waited with us, and then helped us carry our luggage into the car. It was really heartwarming.
Finally, I would like to recommend the hotel‚Äôs catering, which is really rich and delicious. During the two-day stay, the breakfast is not repeated. Although it is included in the room rate, the ingredients are of high quality and rich and varied, except for the designated dishes. style, there are two staple foods to choose from, and there are also some self-service staple foods and soups, coffee, Western-style buns and meat sausages, sumptuous and delicious high-end restaurants, by the way, the hotel's paid dinner, although It‚Äôs a simple meal, but not enough to satisfy you at all. It‚Äôs delicious!!
All in all, this was a very good stay experience, excellent in every aspect, and worthy of staying again.

From the moment I made the reservation, I felt the meticulous service from the hotel butler. They will confirm the itinerary through WeChat in advance and provide detailed taxi location information. When we arrived at the hotel, the enthusiastic guy was already waiting there and took the luggage to the door of the hotel on a tricycle. This thoughtful way of greeting makes people feel warm.
After entering the hotel, the waiter will bring you hot towels and rich refreshments, allowing you to take a moment to rest during the journey. At the same time, the luggage has been delivered to the room quickly, and the entire check-in process is very smooth, showing the hotel's efficiency and attentiveness.

In addition, the hotel's afternoon tea and breakfast are also very rich and of high quality, demonstrating the hotel's dedication and pursuit of quality. Although the room is not large, it has a reasonable layout and returns to the essence of a hotel, providing an excellent sleeping experience. The buckwheat hull pillow, in particular, is one of the most comfortable pillows I have ever slept on.
When leaving, the hotel also gave me a souvenir, and the little brother even helped deliver the luggage to the roadside outside the ancient city, and kept chatting with me until the vehicle arrived. This consistent warm service left a deep impression on me at Anyu Hotel.
In general, although the Anyu Hotel is small in size, it has excellent quality and attentive service. Whether it is the location, room facilities or service attitude, everyone is very satisfied. This stay experience made me full of expectations for Anyu Hotel.

msg:Anyu Ancient City and Anyu are two stores. I live in the ancient city of Anyu. On the first day when I first came in, because garbage trucks would occasionally pass by the alleys entering the hotel, there was a house next to the hotel under renovation, and there was a public toilet next to the hotel, I felt a psychological gap, wondering if it was worth the money.
Later I found out that the money spent was really worth it! This brand can really be praised. ‚ú®I think this is largely due to the service mind of their entire team. It can be said that this team has changed the scene here, and all members must praise it.
First, there is the pick-up or drop-off service. 5 to 10 minutes before arriving at the store, there will be a little brother to greet the guests at the intersection. Because the road in the ancient city is an uneven stone road, it is difficult to walk. The little brother will use a tricycle with a cushion to help guests transport their luggage to the hotel.
On the first day, we were not allocated a room on the second floor because there were guests staying for an extended period of time. Although it was facing the street, it was not as noisy as expected. There will also be considerate turndown service at night, that is, staff will help you close the windows facing the street, so that the outside cannot see the inside.
It can be seen from the room that the whole team is very careful in the layout, trying to organically combine the various needs of the guests with the ancient buildings. In addition, the brand of daily necessities (you can choose Oshudan or Lelabo), hair dryer (Dyson), The choice of bedding and so on makes you feel the hotel's intentions. The hotel also thoughtfully prepared a reusable bag, which contains umbrellas, sunglasses, band-aids, and because the temperature in Lijiang is low, there are also blankets. Although they are also items that cannot be taken away, they really make people feel very warm.
What touched me the most was that we had to travel the next day and couldn't have breakfast. The young lady prepared a full breakfast for us to bring, and it was almost midnight when we asked for it, so we basically responded to our requests.
Then we wanted to change to a room on the second floor. At that time, people were outside, and the hotel staff also helped us pack our luggage and complete the room change.
After moving to the second floor, I saw the snow mountain! Really worthwhile trip ah!
The breakfast is amazing. The bird's nest and sea cucumber are served, and the rice noodle wonton stew is optional. Although the eight side dishes are served in small plates, the taste is very authentic. There are other buffet items to choose from.
There was also a souvenir from An Yu when checking out, and the little brother escorted me all the way, and I felt very heartwarming again.
During this process, we especially want to praise Allie, she is very enthusiastic and sincerely serves the guests. Of course, the staff on those two days were great. Thank you very much for your hard work in serving everyone!
